                              Rate Rate at which amounts of the local currency are converted to the foreign
                              currency.
                              Technical info: alphabetic field, DB field: xwaehr.kurs

                              Factor The rate multiplied by the factor provides the actual rate. The field can
                              be used to exchange information with FinAc.
                              Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xwaehr.faktor

                              Min. CU Smallest currency unit, e.g. 0.01 EUR.
                              Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xwaehr.min_we

                              Rounding Rounding type:
                              • None:
                                 There is no rounding.
                              • Comm:
                                 The number will be rounded commercially.
                              • Up:
                                 The number will be rounded up.
                              • Down:
                                 The number will be rounded down.
                              Technical info: toggle field, DB field: xwaehr.we_rund

                              Euro fact. Conversion rate for the EURO.
                              Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xwaehr.eurokurs

                              Disc. Currency is discontinued. A discontinued currency can no longer be se-
                              lected in the market partner. The currency may remain in orders and on invoic-
3.0 / 02-2023




                              es, however. If a document is processed again, you will then be asked to
                              change the discontinued currency.

                                       Cash Discount Groups
                                       Master Data > Keys > System > Cash Discount Groups > Cash Discount
                                       Groups




                                       Fig. B-108   Cash Discount Groups


                                       You create the cash discount groups to which you can assign market partners
                                       on this dialog. The groups are available in sales and purchasing and can be
                                       changed there.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       Payment condition Display of the key number. To create a new cash dis-
                                       count group, enter the next free number.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xxxskonto.zahlbed

                                       Tpe Description of the cash discount type. Any text can be entered here.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: xxxskonto.art

                                       Month With this field, you control how many (full) months are added to the in-
                                       voice date or to the due date.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xxxskonto.monat

                                       Deadline 1 If necessary, an additional deadline can be added. Example: in-
                                       voice date 02/14, month = 1, deadline = 15 days:
                                       02/14 + 1 month = 03/14
                                       03/14 + 15 days = 03/29
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xxxskonto.frist1

                                       Creation date1-3/Deadline 2 The creation dates (Creation date 1 - Creation
                                       date 3) and Deadline 2 enable an extension of the validity period for the cash
                                       discount. These fields do not always have to be filled in. The creation date 30
                                       corresponds to the last day of the month.
                                       Example:
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       Invoice date 02/10, month = 1, deadline = 10 days, creation date 1 = 15, cre-
                                       ation date 2 = 30:
                                       02/10 + 1 month = 03/10


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                     B-197
                System Keys                                                               Software Reference




                              03/10 + 10 days = 03/20
                              The list of possible invoice creation days refers to 03/31 since starting from 03/
                              20, the next possible creation date is determined.
                              03/31 + 5 days = 04/05
                              This means that the cash discount must be claimed by 04/04.
                              Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: xxxskonto.rechlegtag1-3, frist2

                              Cash Disc. Rate Amount of the cash discount granted in percent.
                              Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xxxskonto.satz

                              Description Defined payment term in words, e.g. 10 days, 2% cash discount.
                              Technical info: alphanumeric field

                              Next Condition The next condition refers to the key for an additional cash
                              discount agreement, which goes into force for the first cash discount agree-
                              ment after the deadline has passed.
                              Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xxxskonto.folgezahlbed
3.0 / 02-2023

                                       Company Allocation
                                       Master Data > Keys > System > Companies/Corporations > Company Alloca-
                                       tion




                                       Fig. B-114     Company Allocation


                                       Here you can assign a company to the individual sites (table xhaus). The data
                                       is then evaluated in all areas (document entry, SA, production) in order to
                                       guarantee the correct site assignment.On this dialog, it is not possible to enter
                                       new sites; it is only possible to make an assignment for existing sites. Please
                                       note that a site without company assignment counts as non-existent.
                                       The dialog is only available if you are using the multi-site function. For addi-
                                       tional information, please contact a service employee of A+W Software Gm-
                                       bH.

                                             Changing the assignment
                                             Since a change of the assignment can have massive consequences for the
                                             document handling in the entire system, there is a security query for each
                                             change, asking whether you really want to do this.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       No Site number. The name is displayed in the next field.

                                       Data > Keys > System > Companies/Corporations).
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: site2comp.compid
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       Customer/Supplier Display of the customer and supplier number. These
                                       count as internal market partners. Internal market partners must absolutely be
                                       maintained in the master data. When opening the dialog for this market partner


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                       B-205
                System Keys                                                                Software Reference




                              in the Master Data > Market Partner menu, the title changes to Internal Market
                              Partner. For internal market partners, it is also possible to store a deviating FI-
                              NAC debtor. However, stricter restrictions apply here: permissible are only in-
                              ternal market partners that belong to the same company/corporate group. If
                              for an internal market partner a deviating FINAC debtor has been entered,
                              then starting from this point, there is also increased checking of the change of
                              the company assignment.
                              The company assignment of an internal market partner cannot be changed if
                              the market partner is also assigned to other internal market partners as FINAC
                              debtor. In this case, the dependency must first be resolved (that is, the FINAC
                              debtor of the affected other internal market partners changed) before a new
                              company assignment can take place.
                              Technical info: display field, DB field: xhaus.kunr/linr

                               Dimension variants
                               Master Data > Keys > Products > Variants > Dims > Dims




                               Fig. B-117   Dimensions


                               All dimension variants are maintained on this dialog, depending on the quan-
                               tity unit. These dimension variants are then assigned in the article master data.
                               The dimension variants are also the basis for the stock management.

                               Descriptions of fields

                               No The variant no. is the unique key within the respective quantity unit (QU).
                               It is used both in the article master data as well as in the course of order entry
                               for identification of the desired variant.
                               Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xxvar.bitnr

                               QU Selection of the quantity unit. The codes are stored on the Quantity Units
                               menu (Codes > System).
                               Technical info: <Selo>, DB field: xxvar.meh

                               Description The description of the dimension variant can be selected at will.
                               Technical info: alphanumeric field

                               Stock Descr The description of a piece in stock can be selected at will.
                               Technical info: alphanumeric field
3.0 / 02-2023




                               Part.Dims 1-3 Length, width, and height are specified in the smallest sensi-
                               ble unit. They are shown automatically during order entry.



                B-214                                                             A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                       Product Keys




                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xxvar.mas1, mas2, mas3

                                       Total Dims The total dimension provides the total dimension of the variant in
                                       the respective system basic unit. In the order entry, the total dimension is cal-
                                       culated using the conversion factor entered here.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xxvar.faktor

                B-218                                                            A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                            Product Keys




                                       Exchange/Additional Rules
                                       Master Data > Keys > Products > Exchange/Additional Rules




                                       Fig. B-121    Exchange/Additional Rules


                                       The Exchange/Additional Rules menu element allows the storage of custom-
                                       er-specific rules according to which the BOM can be added to and parts ex-
                                       changed for individual articles or article types. Here, on the left side of the
                                       dialog, the article or article type is selected for which the rule specified on the
                                       right side of the dialog applies.
                                       The dialog consists of the tabs:
                                       •     Exchange/Additional Rules
                                       •     Details
                                       •     Test Mode

                                       Description of the fields in the Applies to... area

                                       CustArtNo If the CustArtNr field is filled, the rule is only evaluated during en-
                                       try if the entry of the item is done via the customer article. Even if there is inci-
                                       dentally a unique assignment for the A+W Enterprise article and customer.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kuaz.kuartnr

                                       ProdTyp The field is filled with the article type from the header article. The
                                       field does not absolutely have to be filled, but only if the rule is to be applied
                                       specifically for the article type.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kuaz.prodtyp

                                       Product The field is filled with the header article. The field does not absolutely
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       have to be filled, but only if the rule is to be applied specifically for the article.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kuaz.prodnr



                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                           B-219
                Product Keys                                                                   Software Reference




                               1x With the checkbox, you control whether the rule is applied just once or al-
                               ways.
                                The rule is applied just once in the product. This way, it is possible that in
                               the IG a float e.g. 110005 is replaced with a processed float 150005, even if
                               this processed float itself has the article 110005 in the article's BOM. Then no
                               exchange rules will be applied.
                                The rule is always applied.
                               Technical info: toggle field, DB field: kuaz.einmal

                               Atyp The Atyp field is an alternative field that specifies which part should be
                               exchanged or where an article gets an additional element or an element is re-
                               moved.
                               Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kuaz.atyp

                               Article The Article field is an alternative field that specifies which article
                               should be exchanged or where an article gets an additional element or an el-
                               ement is removed. Here, you can describe the rule more generally through
                               special defined details. Thus the rule applies for all FD articles (article type 100
                               to 175) if there is a -1 in this field. For all FM articles without LAMI (article types
                               100 to 160), for -2, and FM articles without LAMI, TG, and fire protection (arti-
                               cle types 100 to 140) with -3.
                               Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kuaz.artnr

                               AP Filling out the Assembly Position field has enormous significance. Espe-
                               cially for glass articles or spacers. This entry has to correspond to the entries
                               for AP on the right side of the rule. If the exchange should apply generally, re-
                               gardless of the AP within the BOM, then AP on the left side can be omitted.
                               Then, however, the entry should not be made on the right side. Furthermore,
                               it is very important that the assembly position in the master data be well-main-
                               tained. For the exchange of frame articles, it is absolutely necessary to specify
                               an assembly position.
                               Technical info: numeric field, DB field: kuaz.orgpos

                               Area In the Area field, you specify when a rule should apply: only for a header
                               article or subpart, always or never (empty). E.g. an article Stempel1 should be
                               added in a TG as additional article, but only if the TG is entered as header ar-
                               ticle (not if the TG is component of an IG). Or an article Stempel2 should be
                               added in a TG as additional article, but only if the TG is a component of anoth-
                               er article (not if the TG is entered as header article). The following values are
                               possible:
                               • Only header
                               • Subpart
                               • always
                               • empty.
                               Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kuaz.kopfflag

                               Description of the fields in the The Rule... section
3.0 / 02-2023




                               Article Select the article that should be entered as addition to the BOM or is
                               exchanged as new article or should be deleted.
                               Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kuaz.azartnr


                B-220                                                                A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                         Product Keys




                                       E/A You specify the action with the toggle. The following values are possible:
                                       • E:
                                          Exchange, exchanges one article for another article.
                                       • A: Addition, adds a new article article to the article's BOM (left side).
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: kuaz.azkz

                                       AP The filling out of this field has enormous significance. Especially for glass
                                       articles or spacers. This entry has to correspond to the entries for AP on the
                                       right side of the rule. If the exchange should apply generally, regardless of the
                                       AP within the BOM, then IP on the left side can be omitted. Then, however, the
                                       entry should not be made on the right side. Furthermore, it is very important
                                       that the assembly position in the master data be well-maintained. For the ex-
                                       change of frame articles, it is absolutely necessary to specify an assembly po-
                                       sition. Possible values are:
                                       • 1:
                                           Weather side: pattern to the outside
                                       • 2:
                                           Weather side: pattern to the airspace
                                       • 3:
                                           Inside: pattern to the airspace
                                       • 4:
                                           Inside: pattern to the inside
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: kuaz.orgpos

                                       Structure If a patterned glass was entered, you use the toggle field to control
                                       the structure direction:
                                       • horizontal
                                       • vertical
                                       • diagonal
                                       • none
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: kuaz.strukthb

                                       N1 Required quantity 1. For muntins, the number of vertical muntins is en-
                                       tered here. For surface processings (e.g. edge grinding), the number of edges
                                       is entered here; these are specified as width. For piece processings (e.g. drill-
                                       ings), the number of processings is entered. Shapes require special attention
                                       (edge allocation).
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: kuaz.anz1

                                       N2 Required quantity 2. For muntins, the number of horizontal muntins is en-
                                       tered here. For surface processings (e.g. edge grinding), the number of edges
                                       is entered here; these are specified as height. For piece processings (e.g. drill-
                                       ings), nothing is entered here. Shapes require special attention (edge alloca-
                                       tion).
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: kuaz.anz2

                                       Pt The print ID in this field determines which print ID the article receives in the
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       BOM.
                                       • N:
                                          No


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                         B-221
                Product Keys                                                               Software Reference




                               •  Y:
                                  Yes
                               • S:
                                  Sales-side papers
                               • P:
                                  Production papers
                               Technical info: toggle field, DB field: kuaz.druckkz

                               Pr The field Pr determines whether the article should get an addition identifier
                               in the BOM and thus be incorporated into the price calculation. The variant "O"
                               means that the original identifier is taken over. If the exchanged article was on
                               E/A in the master data BOM due to the price calculation, the new article will
                               inherit the identifier. The following values are possible:
                               • O:
                                   Original identifier is taken over.
                               • Y:
                                   Yes
                               • N:
                                   No, not set.
                               • E:
                                   Exchange, E/A price identifier Exchange
                               • A:
                                   Addition, E/A price identifier Addition
                               Technical info: toggle field, DB field: kuaz.azpreis

                                       Exchange/Additional Rules - Details
                                       Master Data > Keys > Products > Exchange/Additional Rules > <F2>




                                       Fig. B-122     Exchange/additional rules tab, Details tab


                                       On this tab, detailed information about the exchange and additional rules is
                                       displayed.
                                       When creating a rule, you can already specify all processing parameters in-
                                       tended for the article. Next to each parameter field, there is a checkbox so that
                                       you can select whether the parameter in question should be evaluated. This is
                                       very important if, due to an exchange/addition rule an article can also take on
                                       0 as a valid processing dimension (or quantity).

                                             Fields in the bottom section
                                             Depending on the data input, fields and their names can be shown and hid-
                                             den in the bottom section.

                                       Descriptions of fields
                                       The fields in the Applies to..., Interlayer, and Main layer areas are filled with
                                       the data from the Exchange/Additional Rules tab.

                               Test Mode You specify the action with the toggle. The following values are

                               fields in question control whether or not the parameters should be evaluated.

                               Wind Load Vectors
                               Master Data > Keys > Products > Technical Values > Vectors > Wind Load

                               other. They are used especially on coasts or in harbors.

                               the group in question. A combination is not possible.

                               • Central

                               This field is only evaluated if it contains a selection.

                B-252                                                            A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                          Product Keys




                                       Product Encoding
                                       Master Data > Keys > Products > Technical Values > Product Encoding




                                       Fig. B-144    Product Encoding


                                       A declaration of performance reflects the technical features and performance
                                       characteristics of a product structure. To make the management and allocation
                                       easier, you can define rules as to how the products should be reflected in a
                                       declaration of performance. To this end you can define individual codes for
                                       products and their BOMs.
                                       The basic idea is that only certain characteristics and elements of the product
                                       BOM are relevant for the allocation of a declaration of performance (which is
                                       not the case for a spacer as part of an IG unit, for instance). It is therefore pos-
                                       sible to automatically allocate the same declaration of performance to different
                                       products with similar BOMs. The code can be defined for article types (in gen-
                                       eral) or for individual articles with certain BOM elements (specific). Decisive for
                                       the product code is always the item article or its article type.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       Analysis Type Selection of the type:
                                       • Article Type
                                       • Article Number
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: xprodkeyart.prodmerktyp

                                       Number Selection of the article number or article type.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xprodkeyart.prodmerk

                                       Encoded as Selection of the coding:
                                       • Article no.
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       • Art. type




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                         B-253
                Product Keys                                                              Software Reference




                               The coding means that an exchange of frame articles in the BOM results in the
                               same product codes and no new DP is required. The coding should be created
                               according to the individual operation's specifications. The more precisely the
                               key is coded, the more DPs are required.
                               Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xprodkeyart.prodtypkz

                               General info The fields in this area must be viewed together. We will try to
                               explain this using three examples:
                               • Example 1: for all float glass, the same declaration of performance should
                                  apply (e.g. DP-FLOAT-STD). For this, make the following settings: type of
                                  evaluation - article type, number = 100, encoded as = A-type; all other fields
                                  remain empty.
                                  This way, all products of the article type = 100 (FLOAT fixed size) will get
                                  the product code "|100-<Ass.Pos>". The appropriate declaration of perfor-
                                  mance can now be assigned to this product code.
                               • Example 2: If encoding as Article number is chosen for article type 150
                                  (tempered glass), every tempered glass article will get the product code
                                  "|<Article number>-<Assembly position>" (e.g. "|350005-1" or "|350006-
                                  1").
                                  If a different declaration of performance is required for a special tempered
                                  glass processing, this processing can be defined in Detailed information ei-
                                  ther as the article type, A+W processing type, or as an article number, and
                                  the appropriate encoding type for this processing can be defined. For ex-
                                  ample, a coating with ArtNo. 198160 can become part of the product code
                                  as article number. In this case, product code "|350005-1|198160|" is gen-
                                  erated for tempered glass with this coating.
                               • Example 3: If you select General information > All glass types, all elements
                                  of the BOM with article type 100 to 170 will be included in the code. For IG
                                  articles, the AIR can be included in the code as well as other BOM ele-
                                  ments that are decisive for determining the technical values. In Detailed in-
                                  formation you can also enter specific glass types if not all glass glass types
                                  are important for assigning the declaration of performance.
                               Technical info: toggle field, DB field: xprodkeyart.allgl/typkzallg/allszr
3.0 / 02-2023

                Software Reference                                                                        Product Keys

                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xprodkeyart.merk1

                                       • A-type

                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xprodkeyart.typkz1

                               Motif Assignment
                               Master Data > Keys > Products > Motifs




                               Fig. B-155   Motif Assignment


                               All motif files that are used for surface processing are stored here. The motif
                               must exist in the form of an image file (jpg, png, bmp, gif, tif(s) are supported).
                               You can dimension the motif with the dimension types of the processing type
                               Surface and thus place it on the lite. When opening, the dimensions of the im-
                               age file are taken over 1:1. The width or height of the motif can be adjusted
                               taking the side ratio into consideration. The motif can then be output on the
                               sketches and the printout.

                               Descriptions of fields

                               Number Number of the motif to be described. To create a new motif, enter the
                               next free number.
                               Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xsiebnr.siebnr

                               Description Description of the motif.
                               Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: xsiebnr.siebname

                               Max.width Width of the motif in mm.
                               Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xsiebnr.maxbreite

                               Max.hgt Height of the motif in mm.
                               Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xsiebnr.maxhoehe

                               File Selection of the motif file.
                               Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xsiebnr.dateiname

                               File If you press this button, the document assignment opens, where you can
3.0 / 02-2023




                               drag a selected file when the mouse button is pressed.

                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                        B-291
                Article                                                                  Software Reference




                          Article
                          Master Data > Article
                          Article master data includes all data describing article features and properties.
                          This data represents the product in question and influences a wide variety of
                          areas (e.g. order entry, production, stock, etc.).
                          The data recorded in the article master data provides essential information
                          about the
                          •   Qualities
                          •   Availability
                          •   Feasibility for production
                          •   Accounting estimation
                          •   Spatial dimensions
                          •   Application
                          •   Identification
                          •   For allocation/classification (in groups, type, etc.) of an article.
                          This chapter provides information on the following subjects:
                          •   “Article header” on page B-293
                          •   “Identification” on page B-296
                          •   “Physical Properties” on page B-302
                          •   “Size Restrictions” on page B-307
                          •   “Assembly Restrict.” on page B-309
                          •   “Supplies” on page B-311
                          •   “Production” on page B-314
                          •   “Prices” on page B-318
                          •   “Stock” on page B-322
                          •   “Technical Values” on page B-324
                          •   “Statistics” on page B-326
                          •   “Modifications” on page B-328
                          •   “Private” on page B-329
                          •   “Article - context menu” on page B-294
3.0 / 02-2023

                                       Article header
                                       On this dialog, you can select an article in order to examine or change the ar-
                                       ticle data or you can assign a number to a new article.
                                       <F6> provides the next free number for the article entry from the appropriate
                                       number range. If you assign the new article number according to particular cri-
                                       teria, e.g. by article type, you have to assign the number yourself. For new en-
                                       try, you can use a sample article. The program will help lead you with a
                                       message. You can then change the necessary fields.
                                       The contents of the individual tabs always relate to the article selected in the
                                       header.




                                       Fig. B-170   Article - header


                                       Article Selection of the article number with <F9>. Every article is clearly iden-
                                       tified by its article number. An article number can only be assigned once. The
                                       main article name appears next to the field in plain text. For the newly entered
                                       article without sample article, the name is only displayed after initial sasving.
                                       Technical info: mandatory field, numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.artnr
                                       The dialog offers various tabs. The contents of the individual tabs can - de-
                                       pending on the selection and configuration - be different.

                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                                   B-295
                Article                                                              Software Reference




                          Identification
                          Master Data > Article > Identification




                          Fig. B-171   Article - identification


                          The most important criteria are assigned to an article on the Identification tab.
                          Use <F5> to open a dialog on which you can store note texts for the article.
                          Use <Shift><F5> to open a dialog on which you can store product note texts
                          for the market partner.
                           “Article - Notes” on page B-300

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Matchcode The article matchcode makes it easy to find an article in the sys-
                          tem. The matchcode has to be entered when you define a new article. This can
                          be an article name consisting of letters and numbers. The matchcode can be
                          the same for several articles.
                          Technical info: mandatory field, alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.artmc

                          Article Code This field serves to store an additional, customer-specific name
                          (is used frequently in Asia).
                          Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.artikelcode

                          Main Description The description or name of the article is entered here. The
                          main name of the article appears at order entry, on printouts, etc.
                          When you have entered an article, the main description will appear next to the
                          field Article and, in the SELO search, next to the article number.
                          Use <F5> to open the Article names dialog. You can enter other and foreign-
                          language descriptions for the article there.
3.0 / 02-2023




                           “Other Article Descriptions” on page B-361
                          Technical info: mandatory field, alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.artbez1



                B-296                                                       A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       Int.Descr. These fields are where you can enter internal descriptions of the
                                       article. If you import the article via the BME CAT interface, the manufacturer's
                                       article description is taken over in this field.
                                       You can search for this description in connection with the extended article
                                       search.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.artbez2, artikel.artbez3

                                       Short Name If you want to print a short description of the article on papers
                                       that offer only little space (e.g. labels), you can enter this in the Short Name
                                       field.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.kurzbez

                                       Prod. Group Every article has to be allocated to a product group. The prod-
                                       uct group defines the article price and is the basis for statistical analysis. You
                                       can keep product group-related statistics.
                                       Product groups are defined in: Master data > Products Groups.
                                        “Product groups” on page B-399
                                       Technical info: mandatory field, alphanumeric field, <F9>, DB field:
                                       artikel.wagrp

                                       Description The selected product group is displayed in plain text here (not
                                       selectable).
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: wargrp.wgrbez

                                       Art. Type You have to select the article type for your article here.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • Part:
                                          Parts are all A+W Enterprise articles that describe physical material. There
                                          is no distinction here between header part (product) and sub-part.
                                       • Meta-part:
                                          Meta-parts are all A+W Enterprise articles that provide better legibility or
                                          simplified handling of BOMs. And also parts that serve to bring formulas
                                          into existing BOMs.
                                       • Processing:
                                          For the article, this is a processing, for example cutting, edge grinding, dis-
                                          posal, etc.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.teilflag

                                       Processing Type If you have chosen Processing in field Article type, you
                                       have to select the processing type now. The processing type influences prices
                                       and conditions as well as the definition of corners and edges at order entry.
                                       The field determines the structure of the processing vector.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • -- (empty):
                                          This article is a miscellaneous processing such as drilling, disposal, freight,
                                          etc.
                                       • Corners:
3.0 / 02-2023




                                          This is a corner processing such as a cut-out.
                                       • Edges:
                                          This article is edgework such as edge grinding.


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                        B-297
                Article                                                                  Software Reference




                          •  Facettes:
                             This is a facetting article.
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.ekflag

                          Art. Type The article type must be selected in this field. The selected article
                          type will be displayed next to the field in plain text. An article type combines
                          articles of the same type (and sizes).
                          The article type is necessary to apply exchange/addition rules correctly and to
                          run restriction checks and pricing.
                          During the exchange, for example, it is checked which article types of the
                          same value can be exchanged in the BOM; the system will issue a message
                          if they do not match.
                          This will prevent, for example, that a glass is replaced by a muntin at order en-
                          try.
                          If you search for an article with <F9> or <F8> and enter a start value for the
                          article type, the article type will be sorted by name, not by number.
                          Technical info: mandatory field, <F9> DB field: artikel.atyp

                          A+W Proc. Type You can select the A+W standard processing type in this
                          field if you have selected Processing in the Article type field. The A+W stan-
                          dard processing catalog is a binding standard for the description of processing
                          data for the A+W programs. The standard A+W processing catalog defines for
                          all products the processing steps that can be handled, and the parameters de-
                          scribing them.
                          The selected processing type appears next to the field in plain text.
                          A+W Enterprise will run a feasibility check and inform the user if the A+W Proc.
                          Type does not match the Article type.
                          After selecting the processing type, the Article sizes dialog appears. You can
                          enter size parameters on this dialog.
                           Software Reference, “Article Sizes – Size parameters” on page B-346
                          Technical info: mandatory field, numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.awtyp

                          Fitting Type You can select the fitting type for fittings in this field (article type
                          Fittings). The selected fitting type appears next to the field in plain text.
                          Fitting types are created in Master data > Keys > Products > Fitting types.
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.btyp

                          Spacer Type In this field, you can select the spacer type for spacers and IG
                          spacers (Article Type Spacer or IG Spacer).
                          Selection of the spacer type at document entry will influence the display of the
                          glass structure: different spacer types are shown in different colors.
                          The following options are available for selection:
                          • Steel:
                             The spacer is a steel spacer.
                          • Alu:
                             The spacer is an aluminum spacer.
                          • TPS:
3.0 / 02-2023




                             The spacer is a thermoplast spacer (TPS).




                B-298                                                          A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                   Article




                                       Spacer types are created in the Master Data > Keys > Products > Spacer
                                       Types.
                                        “Description for Spacer Types” on page B-265
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.rtyp

                                       Sealing Type You can select the sealing type for the sealants (Article Type
                                       240) in this field.
                                       Sealing types are created in the Master Data > Keys > Products > Sealing
                                       types.
                                        “Descriptions for Sealing Types” on page B-267
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.versiegelungstyp

                                       Foil Type You can select the foil type for the foils (Article Type foils) in this
                                       field.
                                       Foil types are created in the Master Data > Keys > Products > Foil Types.
                                        “Description for Foil Types” on page B-263
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.folienstyp

                                       EAN Code A valid barcode for the article can be entered here.
                                       Throughout Europe, the EAN code serves to identify articles and their alloca-
                                       tion to article groups, product groups, or product areas. The first two digits of
                                       the 13-digit code identify the country of origin; the next 5 digits, the uniform fed-
                                       eral operation number (bbn); the next 5, the individual article number of the
                                       manufacturer, and the last number serves as a check digits.
                                       You only have to enter the first twelve digits; the system will determine the
                                       check digit.
                                       The EAN code appears on printouts, such as labels.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.eancode

                                       Misc. Product Here you can specify if this is a small part. The article text of
                                       Miscellaneous Products can be changed at document entry. It will get a new
                                       BOM number for every item at document entry. This way, you do not need a
                                       special article number for every small part.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • no:
                                          This is not a miscellaneous product.
                                       • yes:
                                          This is a miscellaneous product.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.tmpartkz

                                       Notes If notes on articles have been entered, they will appear here.


                                       Additional information
                                        “Article - Notes” on page B-300
                                        “Market Partner - Note texts” on page B-23

                          Article - Notes
                          Master Data > Article > Notes <F5>




                          Fig. B-172    Article - Notes


                          On this dialog, you can store texts for articles; these serve as important infor-
                          mation in various parts of the program. At the top of the dialog, you see the
                          article number for which the text applies.

                              Multilingual notes
                              Since QR2209, you can also store multilingual names in A+W Enterprise
                              for Notes . However, this is only possible if you are working with the multi-
                              lingualism for employees within the internal client separation module.

                          Language Language ID.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: xsprbez.sprkz
                          Enter the text in the free field and store it with <F3>.
                          Use <Shift><F9> to specify the info location:
                          •   Master data:
                              The text is only displayed in the master data.
                          •   Everywhere
                              Text appears in the master data and in the sales and purchasing docu-
                              ments if this article is entered as an item. Or if it was marked in the Element
3.0 / 02-2023




                              field with yes/with note.




                B-300                                                         A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                   Article




                                       •     SA order:
                                             Text appears in sales documents if the article is entered as an item. Or if it
                                             was marked in the Element field with yes/with note.
                                       •     PU order:
                                             Text appears in purchasing documents if the article is entered as an item.
                                             Or if it was marked in the Element field with yes/with note.
                                       Use <Shift><F10> to specify the priority:
                                       •     high:
                                             The text is displayed automatically in the specified info locations as soon
                                             as just one line has the Prio=high.
                                       •     low:
                                             The text will not be displayed automatically; it has to be loaded via menu at
                                             document entry.

                                             Priority of info position master data
                                             If you have selected Master data as Info position, the priority low is invalid.
                                             The text always appears in article master data.

                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                           B-301
                Article                                                                 Software Reference




                          Physical Properties
                          Master Data > Article > Physical Properties tab




                          Fig. B-173    Article - Physical Properties tab


                          The physical properties of an article are defined on the Physcal Properties tab.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Shape If the article is a shape, you can select a shape from the shape catalog
                          here.
                          After selecting a shape you can use <F5> to open the Shape parameters dia-
                          log to enter the article sizes.
                          Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.modell

                          QU You must select a quantity unit for the article in this field. The selected
                          quantity unit appears next to the field in plain text.
                          At item entry, the quantity unit controls the type and number of parameters to
                          be entered to describe the product completely. If the selected quantity unit is
                          Area, the system will ask for the width and height of the article at document
                          entry; if it is Linear meters, the length, etc.
                          The selected quantity unit also influences the calculation of weight, pricing,
                          cost calculation, and stock withdrawals.
                          The appropriate units are stored on the Quantity Units menu (Master Data >
                          Keys > System).
                          Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.me

                          Weight The weight per quantity unit can be entered in this field. This informa-
                          tion is important for the calculation of the total weight in the order entry and for
                          dispatch, packaging planning, and discount determination.
3.0 / 02-2023




                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.gew




                B-302                                                         A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                 Article




                                       Product Weight In this field, you can define whether all BOM elements
                                       should be used to determine the product weight, or only the weight of this ar-
                                       ticle.
                                        Only this article serves to determine the weight.
                                        The total weight of all BOM elements will be calculated.
                                       If you activate the checkbox, you can achieve with an additional system con-
                                       figuration that the product weight flows into the calculation nevertheless, inso-
                                       far as this article is exchanged into the BOM.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.produktgew

                                       Thickness Enter the article thickness in mm. Based on this size, the ma-
                                       chines for production control and packaging planning will be selected, and
                                       prices will be calculated for certain processing steps. Likewise, the thickness
                                       is used to calculate the technical values and the thickness of the IG units.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.staerke

                                       Milling Depth The field is only active if the article is a muntin. Then enter the
                                       milling depth of the muntins in mm.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB info: artikel.fraestiefe

                                       Trim The field is only active if the article is a muntin. Then enter the trim value
                                       of the muntins in mm.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB info: artikel.trim_wert

                                       Profile Thickness The field is only active if the article is a muntin. Then enter
                                       the profile thickness of the muntins in mm.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB info: artikel.dicke

                                       Dimens. Variant In this field you can determine whether this article is only
                                       available in particular size variants:
                                        There are size variants for this article.
                                        There are no size variants for this article.
                                       If you choose Size variants, use <F5> to go to the Variants dialog. You can
                                       define size variants there and enter the supply criteria on another dialog.
                                        “Size variants” on page B-335
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.varflag

                                       Color/Size Variant Defines whether color or size variants can be entered for
                                       this article.
                                       • Colors:
                                           The article is available in particular colors.
                                       • Sizes:
                                           The article is available in particular sizes.
                                       • – (none):
                                           No selection was made or Size Variant was selected.
                                       If you choose Colors or Sizes, use <F5> to go to the Colors/sizes dialog.
                                        “Size variants” on page B-335
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       You can enter color or size variants on this dialog and define the supply criteria
                                       on another dialog.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.farbflag


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                         B-303
                Article                                                                Software Reference




                          Surface In this field, you can enter details about surface properties of glass.
                          This is essential for the cutting sequence or the direction of a pattern, for ex-
                          ample.
                          • none:
                             The glass has no special surface.
                          • Pattern one side:
                             The glass has a pattern on one side.
                          • Structure two sides:
                             The glass has a pattern on both sides.
                          • Coating:
                             The glass is coated.
                          • R/L reference:
                             The glass has a pattern whose direction or structured side has to be taken
                             into account for processing.
                              The lite cannot be turned!
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.strukseite

                          Pattern If you select a Pattern or R/L reference in the Surface field, you can
                          define the direction of pattern or the patterned side.
                          • vert:
                             Vertical sense of pattern.
                          • horizontal:
                             Horizontal sense of pattern.
                          • diag:
                             Diagonal sense of pattern.
                          The following options are available for R/L reference for side-related articles:
                          • right:
                             Sense of pattern to the right.
                          • left:
                             Sense of pattern to the left
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.strukhb

                          AssemPos If you have selected in field Surface a Coating, Pattern or R/L
                          reference, you can now enter the fitting position of the glass within the spacer.
                          The assembly position is determined acc. to the following illustration.


                          outside          inside


                                1 2 3 4




                          Fig. B-174   Assembly position of the glass
3.0 / 02-2023




                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.einbaupos




                B-304                                                       A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                  Article




                                       Position to AIR If you enter an IG unit with a coated or patterned lite, you
                                       have to define the assembly direction for this pattern.
                                       • Pointing away from AIR:
                                          The coated/patterned side is on the outside of the IG unit.
                                       • To the AIR:
                                          The patterned/coated surface faces the airspace.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.einbauposstkl

                                       Sales Article In this field, you can specify whether or not the article is for sale
                                       (individual sale).
                                       • Yes:
                                           The article itself can be sold on. It can be entered as an item in document
                                           entry.
                                       • No:
                                           This article is not to be sold as it is. It cannot be entered as an item in doc-
                                           ument entry. It can be included in a BOM, however.
                                       • +Online:
                                           This article can be sold on the Internet.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.verkart

                                       BOM In this field, you can specify whether or not a BOM exists for this article.
                                       • no:
                                           This article has no BOM.
                                       • yes/changeable:
                                           This article has a BOM. You can make changes to the BOM in the docu-
                                           ment entry. For example, you can add or replace articles in the BOM.
                                       • yes/rigid:
                                           This article has a BOM. You cannot make any changes to the BOM in the
                                           document entry.
                                       If you select 'BOM yes', you can use <F5> to open the BOM dialog for further
                                       entries.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.stklst

                                       Sub-Part In this field, you can select whether the article may appear in anoth-
                                       er's article BOM:
                                       • no:
                                           This article cannot be a BOM sub-part.
                                       • yes:
                                           This article can be a BOM sub-part.
                                       • yes/statistics-relevant:
                                           The article must occur as sub-part of a BOM. The article is included in the
                                           part use statistics.
                                       • yes/with note:
                                           This article can be a BOM sub-part. If a note has been entered for this ar-
                                           ticle, it will appear at document entry.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.uteil
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       BOM Replacement If you select yes in the Sub-Part field, you can use this

                                        This article can be replaced by another in a BOM.

                Article                                                               Software Reference




                           This article cannot be replaced by another in a BOM.

                                       Assembly Restrict.
                                       Master Data > Article > Assembly Restrict. tab




                                       Fig. B-176   Article - Assembly Restrict. tab


                                       On the Assembly Restrict. tab, you can define the processing restrictions for
                                       the article. The user will be informed should the defined limit or the assembly
                                       rule is not met at document entry.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       Maximum Drill Diam. In this field, you can enter the maximum drilling diam-
                                       eter for the article.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.maxbohrdm

                                       Minimum Drill Diam. In this field, you can enter the minimum drilling diame-
                                       ter for an article.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.minbohrdm

                                       Mount only if These fields allow you to enter a valid formula for the assem-
                                       bly restrictions. You can combine two restrictions with AND or OR.
                                       In the first and third fields, you can use <F9> to select a valid variable. After
                                       that, an operator is set in these fields next to the variable and a value is input.
                                       The following operators and comparison operators can be set:
                                       • + Addition
                                       • – Subtraction
                                       • * Multiplication
                                       • / Division
                                       • = equal
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       • < less than
                                       • > greater than
                                       • <= less than or equal to


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                        B-309
                Article                                                                  Software Reference




                          •   >= greater than or equal to
                          •   != unequal
                          •   & logical and
                          •   and logical and
                          •   | logical or
                          •   or logical or
                          •   ! logical negation
                          •   not logical negation
                          •   max (x, y) the greater value of the two
                          •   min (x, y) the lesser value of the two
                          •   pi constant Pi (3.415926)


                              Example

                              Muntins must be fitted only if the airspace of an IG unit is at least 16
                              mm and no bigger than 20 mm.
                              In the first field, select variable AIR ($3) for the airspace.
                              After variable $3, add the operator <= for less than or equal to. Now
                              enter the value 20.
                              The formula in the first field would now look as follows: $3<=20.
                              The formula in the third field would be $3>=16.
                              Now combine the formulas in the second field by the link AND.
                              This means that the airspace must be at least 16 mm (or bigger) but
                              no bigger than 20 mm (or less).

                              Exchange field contents
                              In this example, it would not matter if the contents of the first and third field
                              were exchanged.

                          Technical info: 1. and 3. field: alphanumerical fields, <F9>, DB fields:
                          artikel.ebrestrikt1, artikel.ebrestrikt2
                          2nd field: toggle field, DB field: artikel.operator
