                                       Supplies
                                       Master Data > Article > Supplies tab




                                       Fig. B-177   Article - Supplies tab


                                       The Supplies tab is used to enter data regarding the supply of this article.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       Supply Type In the Supply type field, you can select a supply type for the ar-
                                       ticle. The supply types define the priority with which the article is ordered. Pri-
                                       ority 2 will be used if priority 1 is not applicable.
                                       Use <F9> or <F5> to open the Supply types dialog from which you can select
                                       one of the supply criteria with <Enter>.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.beschaffnr

                                       1st, 2nd, 3rd Priority In these fields, the selected combination of the select-
                                       ed supply type from the Supply Type field is displayed in plain text. These
                                       fields describe the priorities for ordering this article.
                                       The selected supply type can be overwritten at document entry.
                                       The following supply types are available:
                                       • Stock:
                                           Article will be taken from stock as long as it is available.
                                       • Order:
                                           Product will be ordered from the supplier.
                                       • Production:
                                           The article will be produced in-house.
                                       • None:
                                           The article is assigned the supply type none. This can be the case for Ar-
3.0 / 02-2023




                                           ticle type Deposit invoice, for example.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric fields



                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                        B-311
                Article                                                               Software Reference




                          Product. Time This field becomes active if one of the first two priorities of the
                          supply type is Production.
                          You can define the production time for the article in working days here. How-
                          ever, the production time does not affect the actual production planning.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.prodzeit

                          Supplier This field becomes active if one of the first two priorities of the sup-
                          ply type is Order.
                          Use <F5> to open the Suppliers dialog. You can enter a standard supplier plus
                          other suppliers there.
                          The standard supplier appears in this field as plain text.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.stdlinr

                          Deliv. Time If you have selected a standard supplier and a delivery time for
                          the article, this field shows the delivery time in days.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.stdlz

                          Purch. Dept. The purchasing departments are stored in the product groups.
                          You can choose another purchasing department here if required. The selected
                          purchasing department appears next to this field in plain text.
                          Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.ekabt

                          E/A supply type If the supply type of an article - as a BOM element - should
                          differ from its supply type as an item, you can make the following settings:
                          • none:
                              No other replacement/addition supply type is selected.
                          • P.O. before EDI
                              The element is ordered from one's own company before the entire BOM is
                              transferred to the producer. The element will be reported as 'included in
                              shipment' to the recipient.
                          • Stock withdrawal before EDI:
                              The element is taken from stock before the entire BOM is transferred to the
                              producer. The element will be reported as 'included in shipment' to the re-
                              cipient.
                          • Production before EDI
                              The element is produced by one's own company before the entire BOM is
                              transferred to the producer. The element will be reported as 'included in
                              shipment' to the recipient.
                          • Order:
                              Product will be ordered from the supplier.
                          • Stock withdrawal:
                              Article will be taken from stock.
                          • Production:
                              The article will be produced in-house.
                          • Included:
                              Article will be delivered from customer to supplier.
                          • Included before EDI:
3.0 / 02-2023




                              Before ordering the article via EDI from another site, the supply type is an-
                              alyzed - the article will be included in the shipment.
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.bestellkz

                          Production
                          Master Data > Article > Production tab




                          Fig. B-178   Article - Production tab


                          The Production tab is used to enter the data for producing this article.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Production Type If a production type was selected as Article Type, you can
                          specify the PMS type in this field. This classifies the article type more precise-
                          ly. This will be analyzed in the production management system (e.g. work pro-
                          cess, etc.).
                          Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.ptyp

                          Cutting Correction You can enter the value in mm for the cutting addition for
                          cut edges here. For example, this may be useful for articles the edges of which
                          should be ground, or for the deduction of edge connections for muntins.
                          In the Formula editor, set field Cutting corr. to Y to perform the cutting correc-
                          tion.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.zkb

                          Muntin Type If the selected Article type is Muntins, you can enter the muntin
                          construction type. Since muntins are cut differently depending on the construc-
                          tion type, the length of the individual muntin bars varies. The Muntin Type de-
                          fines the length of the muntin bars before and after cutting.
                          Muntin types are pre-populated by A+W Enterprise.
                          The following options are available for selection:
                          • 1 = double miter at the intersections
                              An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
3.0 / 02-2023




                              tion).
                          • 2 = continuous miter (1/4 width of the continuous muntin)


                B-314                                                       A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                           - Continuous muntin
                                          An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
                                          tion).
                                       • 3 = blunt connection
                                          – continuous muntin; horizontal muntins bluntly meet the continuous bar.
                                          An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
                                          tion).
                                       • 4 = muntin cross
                                          Horizontal and vertical muntins with blunt connection to the crosspieces. If
                                          a special thickness is defined for a crosspiece (element of the muntin
                                          BOM), this will be used to determine the muntin pattern.
                                          An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
                                          tion).
                                       • 5 = continuous miter (depending on the muntin width)
                                           - Continuous muntin
                                          Fixed miter depths will be used for the muntin width. For a muntin width up
                                          to 45 mm = 7 mm, from 45 mm = 12 mm).
                                          An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
                                          tion).
                                       • 10 = muntin with thermal separating layer
                                          Horizontal and vertical muntins consist of a continuous element (cover,
                                          beam) and elements with a thermal separation layer the length of which
                                          can vary depending on the muntin pattern. We assume that the decisive
                                          muntin width (= width of separation layer) is 6 mm wider than the aluminium
                                          elements.
                                          An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
                                          tion).
                                       • 11 = continuous miter (freely definable)
                                          – continuous muntin with freely definable miter. The miter is defined in
                                          Master data > Article > Private tab > Field 1.
                                          An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
                                          tion).
                                       • 93 = double muntin with blunt connection
                                          Double muntin means that the horizontal muntins bluntly meet the continu-
                                          ous muntins. The meta element muntin consists of two thin muntins. For
                                          the trade, drillings are calculated based on the meta element muntin (thick-
                                          ness). For production, two drill points will be calculated by muntin, based
                                          on the thickness of the sub-elements.
                                          An edge connection can be taken into account at the edges (cutting correc-
                                          tion).
                                       Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.sprtyp

                                       Alternative Type If you have selected a muntin construction type in the
                                       Muntin Type field, you can enter a second type here.
                                       If different muntins are to be fit into an IG unit, A+W Enterprise will check at
                                       order entry whether the types of the muntins are compatible. If not, A+W En-
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       terprise will check if the defined Alternative type is compatible. If not, A+W En-
                                       terprise will issue a message.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.sprfor


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                       B-315
                Article                                                              Software Reference

                          LAMI/CR Inheritance If the selected Article type is Processing for LAMI or

                          Prices
                          Master Data > Article > Prices tab




                          Fig. B-179   Article - Prices tab


                          On this dialog, you specify data for the price calculation of the article. Each ar-
                          ticle is calculated according to a price method that is attuned to the BOM.

                             Price method no longer used

                          In older installations, price methods could be assigned to the articles; these
                          are no longer used in the newer version. If a message to this effect is dis-
                          played, you must change the assignment in the master data.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Price Method Selection of the pricing method. The pricing method controls
                          the price calculation for an article. They are used to determine the prices from
                          the price lists and the conditions. For each product group, there is an individual
                          pricing method, which considers the special properties of the product group in
                          the pricing.
                          • 5 - muntin prices
                          • 7 - processing matrices is no longer used.
                          • 12 - PCd glass doors for all-glass doors, refers to PCd-General Prices.
                          • 22 - PC-TG for TG.
                          • 41 - IG-current for IG units.
                          • 40 - IG-Swiss for the calculation of IG units according to Swiss specifica-
                              tions.
                          • 23 - PCd basic glass for float.
3.0 / 02-2023




                          • 24 - PCd processed glass is no longer used.
                          • 25 - PCd Prices General for other articles whose price is calculated with a
                              price vector. The PCd is not used for glass and color variants.


                B-318                                                        A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       •  26 - PCd Processings for processings whose price is calculated with a
                                          price vector.
                                       • 28 - PCd Glazing, refers to PCd General Prices.
                                       • The last price assigned in the order can be saved for the customer in ques-
                                          tion.
                                       • 31 - PCd Color Article for colored articles and other article variants that are
                                          not glass.
                                       • 60 - UV protection
                                       • 99 - manual prices.
                                       No values are taken over from the conditions. The price has to be entered
                                       manually in the order.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, <F9>, DB field: artikel.vkptyp1

                                       Price Recording The last price assigned in the order can be saved for the
                                       customer in question.
                                       The saved price can then be selected in orders for the same question in the
                                       Price/pc. field. In addition, it also exists in the price information system.
                                        Save the last used price for this customer.
                                        Do not save the last used price for this customer.
                                        Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.preisrec

                                       Price Presentation The price can be printed on the forms. What and where
                                       prices are printed is specified in the report definition that belongs to the form.
                                       The report definitions are defined customer-specifically.
                                       • No price:
                                           The price will not be printed.
                                       • QU price:
                                           The price per quantity unit is printed, e.g. per sqm.
                                       • Piece price:
                                           Print price per unit/piece.
                                       • QU + piece price:
                                           The price per quantity unit and per piece is printed. Technical info: toggle
                                           field, DB field: artikel.poffen
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.poffen

                                       Cost Calculation If you are working with the Cost Calculation module, you
                                       can specify whether costs for the article produced should be calculated.
                                       Here, the costs are only calculated for BOM elements with the supply type Pro-
                                       duction. The header part to whose BOM the article is attached, also has to
                                       have the supply type Production. Please note that the supply type defined in
                                       the order will be analyzed, not that defined in article master data.
                                       • no:
                                          The BOM subpart is not evaluated in the cost calculation. The article BOM
                                          will be searched in descending order for other, cost-relevant articles.
                                       • yes:
                                          This BOM subpart is included in the cost calculation. Material costs will be
                                          calculated based on the production price list. The BOM of this article will
3.0 / 02-2023




                                          not be searched for other, cost-relevant articles.




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                        B-319
                Article                                                                Software Reference




                          •   yes/next:
                              The article costs are calculated based on the production price list. They are
                              incorporated in the costs as an internal contribution margin. The article's
                              BOM is searched in ascending order for additional cost-relevant articles.
                          •   loss/next:
                              The loss refers to the material loss, e.g. due to cutting. It has to be consid-
                              ered during price calculation.
                              The loss is analyzed for all BOM elements if the supply type is Production
                              or Stock and if they are marked as Loss/next and multiplied.
                              You specify the loss as a percentage in the Loss (Material) field.
                               “Loss (Material)” on page B-320

                              Articles with the supply type stock
                              For a stock article, the BOM is never checked. The settings for cost calcu-
                              lation are not considered for these articles. Only the costs of the header ar-
                              ticle are used for cost calculation.

                              Articles with the supply type order
                              For ordered articles, the conditions of the allocated supplier are analyzed.
                              All price-relevant subparts are included in the calculated price.

                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.kostenkalk

                          Cash D.-able You can specify whether a cash discount is granted for the ar-
                          ticle.
                           Cash discount can be granted.
                           No cash discount can be granted.
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.skontokz

                          Loss (Material) Specification of the percentage material loss. The loss of ma-
                          terial is meant as a general surcharge for quantity calculation. It can be applied
                          at will, e.g. for waste.
                          The material loss is considered during the material cost calculation. A loss will
                          be calculated when the article is produced or when stock dimensions are with-
                          drawn from stock.
                          The loss of material affects the quantity used to calculate the unit price based
                          on the quantity unit price. Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.mver-
                          lust

                          Correct. Factor Specification of the calculated loss for the article. The cor-
                          rection factor is meant as a general surcharge for pricing. It can be applied at
                          will, e.g. for waste.
                          The calculated loss leads in the calculation of the order to a price surcharge in
                          % by the specified value.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.kverlust

                          Standard Price Specification of the standard price for the article. This price
                          can be used for individual transfer to financial accounting or for other, individ-
3.0 / 02-2023




                          ual analyses.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.stdpreis



                B-320                                                        A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       Price Type Specification of to what the specified price refers:
                                       • CU/piece:
                                          Price that is calculated per piece.
                                       • CU/BQU:
                                          The price is calculated per basic quantity unit (BQU) from the article master
                                          data, e.g. per square meter, etc.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.preistyp

                                       Material Group Specification of a material group. You can enter any alpha-
                                       numeric code with 2 digits. You can use the material group to create your own
                                       analyses.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.artgrp

                                       Processing Group Specification of the processing group. This makes only
                                       sense if the article is an element or a meta-element with a BOM.
                                       You can enter any alphanumeric code with 2 digits. Upper and lower-case let-
                                       ters are distinguished, e.g. 5H and 5h.
                                       A surcharge can be defined for each processing group. If a price-relevant pro-
                                       cessing step or an element is allocated in the BOM below this article, the basic
                                       price for the processing step or for the element is increased by the defined sur-
                                       charge.
                                       You specify the surcharges on the Processing Surcharges dialog in the pricing
                                       area.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.bearbgrp

                                       Tax Rates Specification of the valid tax rate. This field is active if you are us-
                                       ing several tax rates. You can specify up to 4 tax rates, which are separated
                                       with plus (+). The tax rates are evaluated per item in the order.
                                       The resulting values are summed up in the order footer and are listed per VAT
                                       rate, and in total.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.steuerzu
3.0 / 02-2023




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                       B-321
                Article                                                                Software Reference




                          Stock
                          Master Data > Article > Stock tab




                          Fig. B-180   Article dialog - Stock


                          The Stock tab serves to define the stock data for an article. This tab is acces-
                          sible only if on the Supply tab, one of the supply types (priorities) is Stock. For
                          each article you can define in master data how changes of stock have to be
                          booked. This allows you to map individual company-specific stocks.

                             Variant stock
                             You can define different stocks for variants. If there are entries on the Vari-
                             ants (size variants) dialog, A+W Enterprise will adopt the different stock for
                             the variants.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Default Stock Select the default stock for this article if you have chosen the
                          Supply type Stock. The selected stock appears next to the field in plain text.
                          This stock must be used for all articles to be invoiced in pieces or quantities;
                          no additional information needs to be entered for receipts/withdrawals.
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.laghaus

                          Box Warehouse In this field, you can select the box stock in which the article
                          is located. The selected stock appears next to the field in plain text. Only com-
                          plete boxes of an article (e.g. stock sizes) are entered in the box stock. If only
                          certain lites from a box are required, the whole box is resolved, and the lites
                          are booked to the default stock as individual articles.
                          The box stock must contain only complete boxes.
                          For more information, please see Inventory module > Box withdrawal.
3.0 / 02-2023




                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.kistlnr




                B-322                                                        A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                 Article




                                       Slot Warehouse In this field, you can select the warehouse stock for this ar-
                                       ticle. The selected warehouse appears next to the field in plain text. This ware-
                                       house can be used for all articles invoiced by pieces or quantity. It is split into
                                       individual slots that can be allocated as required. It is essential to allocate a
                                       slot name to the article in question to be able to determine the article's storage
                                       location.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.fachlnr

                                       Change in Stock In this field, you can define when the stock on hand should
                                       be changed for this article.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • none:
                                          There are no stock withdrawals for this article.
                                       • Manual:
                                          Order-related additions to and withdrawals from stock have to be done
                                          manually.
                                       • Delivery note:
                                          Dispatch of goods will be booked automatically when the delivery note has
                                          been issued. This change of stock is impossible for the stack and box
                                          stock.
                                       • Picking:
                                          Stock withdrawal will be booked when the picking list is printed.
                                       • AWP:
                                          Stock withdrawal will be booked when the article has been produced and
                                          the completion report has been made.
                                       • Completion report:
                                          If the system is configured appropriately, the evening stock routine with-
                                          draws the glass automatically from the stock. The data, however remains
                                          unbooked (status=0) until the planned date in the database table wlppms.
                                       • Delivery note/AWP:
                                          Depending on what happens first:
                                          Stock withdrawal will be booked as soon as the delivery note has been is-
                                          sued. Or, the production management system (A+W Production) transfers
                                          the forecast to stock to be used for purchase forecasts. The actual change
                                          of stock is made manually or by means of special interfaces (XTV).
                                          This change of stock is impossible for the stack and box stock.
                                       • Manual/AWP:
                                          Depending on what happens first:
                                          Order-related additions to and withdrawals from stock have to be done
                                          manually.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.bestaend
3.0 / 02-2023




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                        B-323
                Article                                                               Software Reference




                          Technical Values
                          Master Data > Article > Tech. Values tab




                          Fig. B-181   Article - Tech. Values tab


                          On the Tech. Values tab, you can enter technical details (sound protection,
                          heat protection, energy transmission, light transmission) for the article. Each
                          article needs to be classified to be able to determine the technical details. The
                          classification describes a group of glass which, in an IG unit, have the same
                          effect on the corresponding technical detail.
                          Use <Ctrl> + <F8>, depending on the configuration, to open the Technical de-
                          tails dialog to make further entries.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Sound insul. (dB) In this field, you can select the db group for the article. The
                          db group unites glass with identical sound protection properties. This entry
                          serves to determine the sound protection for a certain product structure in
                          which up to three lites can be combined. The selected group appears next to
                          the field in plain text.
                          DB groups are entered in Master data > Keys > Products > Technical details
                          > Groups > Sound protection (dB).
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.dbgrp

                          Thermal insul. (U) In this field, you can select the U group for the article. The
                          U group unites lites with identical heat protection properties. This entry serves
                          to determine the heat protection for a certain product structure in which up to
                          three lites can be combined. The selected group appears next to the field in
                          plain text.
                          U groups are entered in Master data > Keys > Products > Technical details >
3.0 / 02-2023




                          Groups > Thermal properties (U).
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.kgrp



                B-324                                                       A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                  Article




                                       Energy transm. (g) In this field, you can select the g group for the article. The
                                       g group unites lites with identical energy transmission properties. The entry
                                       serves to determine the energy transmission for a certain product structure in
                                       which up to three lites can be combined. The selected group appears next to
                                       the field in plain text.
                                       G groups are entered in Master data > Keys > Products > Technical details >
                                       Groups > Energy transmission (g).
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.ggrp

                                       Light transm. (T) In this field, you can select the T value for this article. The
                                       T group unites lites with identical light transmission properties. The entry
                                       serves to determine the light transmission for a certain product structure in
                                       which up to three lites can be combined. The selected value appears next to
                                       the field in plain text.
                                       T groups are entered in Master data > Keys > Products > Technical details >
                                       Groups > Transmission.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.trgrp

                                       Limits for The wind load for this article is added in this field. Wind load (unit:
                                       N/m²) is the pressure or suction applied by direct winds onto the external sur-
                                       face of a building. The selected value appears next to the field in plain text.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.grenzgrp

                                       Thickn group In this field, you can select the thickness group for this article.
                                       The selected value appears next to the field in plain text. The thickness group
                                       unites lites of the same thickness.
                                       Thickness groups are entered in Master data > Keys > Products > Technical
                                       details > Groups > Thickness.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.dgrp

                                       Cekal In this field, you can specify if the production of this IG unit is controlled
                                       by the independent examination institute Cekal.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • No:
                                          No Cekal code allocated.
                                       • Yes:
                                          A Cekal code is allocated.
                                       • Outside:
                                          Cekal codes are assigned only to the lite on the outside of the IG unit.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artikel.cekal

                                       CE Code In this field, you can enter the CE text to be printed for the article.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.cekz

                                       Declaration of Performance You can specify here whether or not there is a
                                       declaration of performance for the article. If there is, you can enter the appro-
                                       priate declaration of performance in the next field.
3.0 / 02-2023




                                        This article has a declaration of performance.
                                        This article does not have a declaration of performance.
                                       Technical info: checkbox, SELO (<F9>)


                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                          B-325
                Article                                                                Software Reference




                          Statistics
                          Master Data > Article > Statistics tab




                          Fig. B-182   Article Statistics Dialog


                          On the Statistics tab, you can enter statistical data on the article. Analyses can
                          be based on these criteria.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Intrastat In this field, you can enter the Intrastat number. The Intrastat num-
                          ber is a code issued by the Federal Statistical Office to analyze trade between
                          the members of EC countries. It is required for international trading.
                          Intrastat numbers are kept in System > Statistical data > Intrastat.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.intrastat

                          Cat. Classifies the article by its stock turnover or turnover.
                          The following options are available for selection:
                          • A:
                             High
                          • B:
                             Medium
                          • C:
                             Low
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.artart
3.0 / 02-2023




                B-326                                                        A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       Cost Center You can define the cost center for the article in this field. Cost
                                       centers are logical business areas (departments, groups) incurring calculable
                                       costs. The selected cost center is analyzed if an article-related cost center is
                                       required at order entry.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.kostenst

                                       Acc. No. In this field, you can define an account number for the article.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artikel.konto

                                       Analysis Group You can select an analysis group for the article in this field.
                                       The analysis group appears next to the field in plain text. Analysis groups are
                                       used to create individual analyses.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artikel.alysegrp

                                       Article Statistics In this field, you can select whether the article should ap-
                                       pear in the general article statistics. This is useful for introducing a new prod-
                                       uct, to see how it fares on the market. Statistics will inform you of this article
                                       whenever it is sold as a product in an order but not if it is part of a BOM.
                                        Article will appear in article statistics.
                                        Article will not appear in article statistics.
                                       Technical info: checkbox, DB field: artikel.arttist
3.0 / 02-2023

                          Modifications
                          Master Data > Article > Modification tab




                          Fig. B-183   Article Modification Dialog

                          Descriptions of fields

                          time, and when.
                          Technical info: display field, DB fields: artikel.neumanr, artikel.neudatum

                          Modified frm/on These fields show who was the last person to change this
                          article, and when.
                          Technical info: display field, DB fields: artikel.manr, artikel.aenderdat

                          Suppliers – Allocation
                          Master Data > Article > Supplies tab > Suppier field > <F5> or
                          Master Data > Article > <Shift> + <F4> > Supplier




                          Fig. B-185    Supplier allocation


                          On this dialog, you can store details about the supplier for articles with supply
                          type=order.
                          Use <F6> to add more suppliers.
                          Use <F2> to open the Details tab.
                          Use <F5> to define the main supplier.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Supplier In this field, you can name the supplier for the article. The selected
                          supplier appears next to the field in plain text. As soon as an order is executed,
                          the supplier is used.
                          If several suppliers have been entered, you can use <F5> to define the default
                          supplier for this article. The default supplier will be automatically used first for
                          purchasing this article.
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artliefzu.linr

                          P.O. No. In this field, you can define the article number the supplier uses for
                          this article.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artliefzu.exartnr
3.0 / 02-2023




                          P.O. name In this field, you can store the article name that the supplier uses
                          for this article.

                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artliefzu.bestellbez

                                       Price In this price, you can enter the price at which the article is purchased
                                       from the selected supplier. This field will be analyzed only with appropriate
                                       configuration.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artliefzu.preis

                                       Type If you have entered a value in the Price field, enter the quantity unit this
                                       price refers to.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • CU/piece:
                                           Purchase price is calculated per piece.
                                       • CU/BQU:
                                           The price is calculated per basic quantity unit (BQU) from the article master
                                           data, e.g. per square meter, etc.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artliefzu.ptyp

                                       Description of the fields on the Details tab

                                       Time In this field, you can enter the delivery time in calendar days for this ar-
                                       ticle. The time entered will influence purchasing and thus the supplier's pro-
                                       duction planning. It appears at order entry.
                                       If a supplier has been defined as the default supplier, this time appears in field
                                       Delivery time.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artliefzu.liefzeit

                                       Qty In this field, you can enter the standard quantity ordered from this suppli-
                                       er. This quantity will be suggested in connection with the stock. You can over-
                                       ride this quantity in the PO pool.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artliefzu.menge

                                       EAN Code In this field, you can enter the EAN code the supplier uses for this
                                       article.
                                       Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artliefzu.eancode

                          Slot Warehouse In this field, you can enter the slot warehouse to which the
                          delivered quantity should be allocated. The selected warehouse appears next
                          to the field in plain text.
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artfarbzu.fachlnr

                          Price In this field, you can enter the purchase price for this variant.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: artfarbzu.preis

                          Type If you have entered a value in the Price field, enter the quantity unit this
                          price refers to.
                          The following options are available for selection:
                          • CU/piece:
                              Purchase price is calculated per piece.
                          • CU/BQU:
                              The price is calculated per basic quantity unit (BQU) from the article master
                              data, e.g. per square meter, etc.
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artfarbzu.preistyp

                                       You can use the <arrow keys> to move from variable to variable. Use <Enter>

                          Compulsory Dimensions — View 1
                          Master Data > Article > <Shift> + <F4> > Dimensioning > Compulsory Dimen-
                          sions
                          or Size parameter selection dialog > End




                          Fig. B-192   Compulsory Dimensions – View 1 dialog


                             Analyzing the compulsory dimensions
                             Compulsory dimensions are analyzed if the article is sold as an item. Com-
                             pulsory dimensions will not be analyzed if the article belongs to a BOM.

                          The fields on the Compulsory Dimensions dialog are pre-populated from the
                          Size parameter selection dialog.
                          Use <F5> to go to the Size parameter selection dialog. You can define other
                          dimension parameters anytime there.
                          <F2> opens another view. You can enter foreign-language text there. This is
                          necessary if you want to print size parameters on forms, and for master data
                          replication for different languages.
                          Use <F3> to create the dimensions for the selected article type.

                             Define compulsory dimensions for the individual article or for the
                             entire article type!
                             Compulsory dimensions apply to the selected article if only the field Article
                             or also the field Article type have been filled in.

                             If you select only the article type in the Article type field without entering an
                             article, you define the sizes for the entire article type!

                          Descriptions of fields
3.0 / 02-2023




                          Article This field is pre-populated with the article number. For dimensions for
                          an article type, this field is pre-populated with the corresponding article type.
                          Technical info: numeric field, DB field: musskenn.artnr, musskenn.atyp


                B-342                                                         A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       Art. Type Use <F3> in fields $1 — $20 or Value to go to field Article type. You

                                       type.

                                       $1 – $20 These fields show the variables you have selected on the Size pa-
                                       rameter selection dialog. You can override the variable name.
                                       The variable names appear as column headers in the document entry dialogs
                                       above the corresponding input fields and can be included in the item text.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric fields, DB fields: musskenn.txtgv1 – muss-
                                       kenn.txtgv20

                                       Value These fields show the defaults for the variables; they are entered at
                                       document entry. This means that this value is used to pre-populate the param-
                                       eter field at document entry. However, the value can be overwritten. These
                                       fields can also be left empty.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: musskenn.gv1 – musskenn.gv20

                                          ment entry where it can be overridden.

                                       • No:

                                       Article dimensioning - Texts
                                       Master Data > Article > <F4> > Dimensioning > Article Dimensioning > [Text]




                                       Fig. B-196      Article Sizes dialog - [Text] button


                                       On this dialog, you can store dimension parameter descriptions in various lan-
                                       guages.

                                             Multilingualism for internal client separation
                                             If you are working with the Multilingualism for employees within the internal
                                             client separation module, the parameter name for all existing languages
                                             must absolutely be stored in the article master data.

                                       Descriptions of fields on the lower part of the dialog

                                       Add. Text Here you can specify if additional text should be entered. If you
                                       choose variable, fixed or must in the first field, you can enter additional text
                                       in the second field.
                                       Options for the first field are:
                                       • variable:
                                           In the second field you can enter an additional text that will be used at doc-
                                           ument entry and can be changed there.
                                           You can enter any text or formula.
                                       • fixed:
                                           In the second field you can enter an additional text that will be used exactly
                                           as it is at document entry and cannot be changed there.. This has to be
                                           text, no formula.
                                       • must:
                                           In the second field you can enter an additional text that will be used at doc-
3.0 / 02-2023




                                           ument entry and can be changed there.
                                           The additional text has to be entered at document entry at the latest.



                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                         B-349
                Article                                                                Software Reference




                          •  no:
                             No additional text is permitted.
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artvermass.getztxt, artvermass.ztxt

                          Autom. text creation Here you can select whether or not text should be au-
                          tomatically created for this article.
                          The following options are available for selection:
                          • Yes:
                             Processing text for this article is created automatically.
                             The text consists of the Main name and the details entered in the fields De-
                             scription and Default.
                          • No:
                             The processing text consists of the entries in the fields Processing text 1
                             and Processing text 2.
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artvermass.autotxtgen

                          Processing text 1, 2 You can enter a text description for the article in these
                          fields. Autom. text creation has to be N for this purpose.
                          You can use different variables for reference:
                          • $W1 – $W6 contents of the corresponding field Default of Size Parameters
                              1–6
                          • $T1 – Main article name
                          • $T2 – Internal name
                          • $ZT – Additional text
                          • $AP – Price-relevant quantity
                          • $A1 – Qty 1
                          • $A1 – Qty 1
                          • $PR – Price
                          If you choose one of the variables $T1, $T2 or $ZT, you can define the print
                          length for the text. Next to the variable, enter the desired text length in rounded
                          brackets, e.g. $ZT(20) for a 20-character text.
                          The number format for variables the numbers of which are allocated, can be
                          defined in rounded brackets. $PR(5.2) means for example that the price con-
                          sists of a total of five digits two of which are after the colon (***.**). $PR(6.2)
                          would be a total of six digits two of which are after the colon (****.**) etc.
                          Technical info: alphanumeric fields, DB fields: nsteuer.bearbtxt1,
                          nsteuer.bearbtxt2

                          Shape dimensioning

                          from the shape catalog. Depending on which shape you have selected, the
                          shape will be displayed on the Shape sizes dialog.

                          ing sizes.

                          they can be overwritten if necessary.

                          Price Characteristics
                          Master Data > Article > <F4> > Price Characteristics




                          Fig. B-202   Price characteristics


                          You can define price characteristics on this dialog.

                          You can specify the price characteristics for the following:
                          •   Article types
                          •   Article
                          •   A+W processing types
                          •   Combination of article and A+W processing type
                          The price characteristics are then evaluated in this sequence: If an A+W pro-
                          cessing type is present in the article, the records for article type and artical
                          without processing type are not evaluated.

                B-358                                                        A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                    Article




                                       Price Calculation With this checkbox, you control whether the price of indi-
                                       vidual processings should be used for the calculation.
                                        The article is calculated if the exchange/additional flag in the BOM in the or-
                                       der is set to A or Z.
                                        The article is not calculated if the exchange/additional flag in the BOM in the
                                       order is set to A or Z.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artpreiseig.part

                                       Shape Surch. Selection for shape surcharge:
                                        Any existing shape surcharge is calculated.
                                        No shape surcharge is calculated.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artpreiseig.modzukz

                                       Discountable Selection for gross or net flag:
                                        Any existing discount factor is calculated.
                                        The article is always calculated with factor=100.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artpreiseig.brutnetkz

                                       Minim.PriceRel. Selection for minimum price relevance:
                                        The price of the processing is included in the total of the processing price
                                       that is compared to the minimum price.
                                        The processing is calculated normally.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artpreiseig.minprrel

                                             Minimum price-relevant processings
                                             Processings are minimum price-relevant if:
                                             - in article dimensioning it is defined that the price should be calculated, and
                                             the Minimum price-rel. flag is set. (The article must be marked as ex-
                                             change/addition in the BOM to allow pricing.)
                                             - the Minimum processing price field is set to “Y” in general daily conditions
                                             (sales), or in general conditions for a project (sales), a customer, or a cus-
                                             tomer group.
                                             - it is not explicitly defined for the main tempered/laminated article that min-
                                             imum processing prices shall not be applied. In this case, the Minimum pro-
                                             cessing price field must be configured and set to “N”.

                                       Quantity 1 Proposed value for quantity 1.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artpreiseig.defanz1

                                       Quantity 2 Proposed value for quantity 2.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artpreiseig.defanz2

                                       Other Article Descriptions
                                       Master Data > Article > Identification tab > Main Description field > <F5>
                                       Master Data > Article > <F4> > Additional Descriptions




                                       Fig. B-203   Article Descriptions dialog – View 1


                                       On the Descriptions tab, you can enter foreign-language descriptions for the
                                       article.
                                       Depending on the market partner's language, the descriptions will be output in
                                       the partner's language in the report or text generation.
                                       There is another view per language in which you can enter more information.
                                       Place the cursor on the required language and use <F2> to open the second
                                       view for the selected language.
                                       Entries the local language will be loaded automatically from the entries on the
                                       Identification tab.

                                       Description of the fields on the Details tab

                                       Language In the Language field, you can select the language in which the ar-
                                       ticle name should appear. You can enter article names one after another in dif-
                                       ferent languages. The language will affect the text and the printing of article
                                       data.
                                       The language is allocated as a number, and shown in plain text next to the field
                                       Language.
                                       Languages are entered in Master data > Keys > System > Language.

                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artbezfremd.sprkz




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                      B-361

                          Main Description Enter the main article name in the corresponding lan-

                          md.artbez3

                                       Article Texts
                                       Master Data > Article > <F4> > Article Texts > Article Texts




                                       Fig. B-204    Article Texts


                                       Article texts are texts that will be printed on forms in addition to the article in
                                       the item (depending on the selection).

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       No You can enter the sequential number for the article text here. This is im-
                                       portant if you enter more than one article text. These will be sorted by numbers
                                       and printed in this sequence.
                                       Use <F5> to open the Forms dialog. You can define the forms on which the
                                       article text should be printed on this dialog. Your selection appears in the info
                                       line of the Article Text dialog.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artxtzu.lfdnr

                                       File In this field, you can select the file in which the desired text is stored.
                                       To create a new file, enter a file name in this field. Confirm the following ques-
                                       tion "No file of this name! Create this file?" with [Yes].
                                       The Master Texts dialog appears. Or open it with <F3>.
                                       You can now enter new text in different languages, or change existing text.
                                       Use <F5> to open the Forms dialog.
                                       You can define the forms on which the article text should be printed on this di-
                                       alog. Your selection appears in the info line of the open dialog (Article Text,
                                       Customer Article Text, Project Article Text).
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artxtzu.datei

                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                          B-367
                Article                                                               Software Reference




                          Supply Types
                          Master Data > Article > Supplies tab > Supply Type field
                          Master Data > Article > <F4> > Supply Types or
                          Master Data > Article > <F4> > Variants > Supply field > <F9>




                          Fig. B-209   Supply Types


                          You can select a supply type for every article and variant. The supply types de-
                          fine the priority with which the article is ordered.
                          If you have selected supply types for both the article and its variants, the pri-
                          ority of the variants' supply types is higher than that of the article.
                          Depending on the priorities defined, the system will ask for more parameters.
                          If you select Stock for example, you will have to enter a stock number; for P.O.
                          you have to define a supplier, etc.
                          Use <F6> to create a new supply type number, insofar as there is not yet a
                          combination of supply types. You cannot change an existing combination after
                          the fact. Use <F7> to delete supply types that are no longer required.

                          Fields on the Supply Types dialog

                          Number Use <Enter> to choose a supply type.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artbeschaff.beschaffnr

                          Production This field defines if the article is produced on site or not.
                          The following options are available for selection:
                          • yes:
                             Article is produced on site.
                          • no:
                             Article is not produced on site.
                          • yes + i.i.:
                             Article is produced on site and invoiced internally.
3.0 / 02-2023




                          • no + i.i.:
                             Article is not produced on site but invoiced internally.



                B-368                                                       A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artbeschaff.prod

                                       Purchase Defines if the article has to be purchased.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • yes:
                                          Article will be purchased.
                                       • no:
                                          Article will not be purchased.
                                       • yes + i.i.:
                                          Article is purchased and invoiced internally.
                                       • no + i.i.:
                                          Article is not purchased but invoiced internally.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artbeschaff.zukauf

                                       Stock Defines if the article is taken from stock.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • no:
                                          Article is not taken from stock.
                                       • yes:
                                          Article is taken from stock.
                                       • central:
                                          Article is taken from the central stock. The system treats this selection just
                                          like Stock.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artbeschaff.lagteil

                                       Priority 1 Defines the highest priority for supplying this article.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • Stock:
                                          Article will be taken from stock as long as it is available.
                                       • Order:
                                          Product will be ordered from the supplier.
                                       • Production:
                                          The article will be produced in-house.
                                       • None:
                                          The article gets supply priority none. This can be the case for Article type
                                          Deposit invoice, for example.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artbeschaff.beschaffart1

                                       Priority 2 Defines an additional priority for supplying this article. This will be
                                       used if priority 1 is not feasible.
                                       Example: Priority 1: Stock, Priority 2: P.O.
                                       The article is always taken from stock. If there is no stock on hand, a P.O. sug-
                                       gestion will be issued automatically.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artbeschaff.beschaffart2
3.0 / 02-2023

                Article                                                             Software Reference




                          Send article to A+W CAD Designer
                          (Bars)
                          Master Data-> Article-> F4 -> Article Data Comparison ->Send Article to AWD-
                          esign
                          The Send article to AWDesign menu item allows you to send a copy of all ar-
                          ticle master data allocated to Article type Muntins to AWDesign.
                          Furthermore, all muntin types for which Muntin type MACRO has been select-
                          ed, will be transferred.
                          These are saved in a file with a certain format and will be transferred to A+W
                          CAD Designer (Bars).

                             Names in the main language
                             A+W CAD Designer (Bars) is not multilingual. Names will therefore be im-
                             ported only in the main language.

                          Confirm the query "Send articles to AWDesign?" with [Yes]. The prompt shows
                          the message "Unloading muntin articles...".
                          This function is no longer used.

                          Replication Data
                          Master Data > Article > <F4> > Article Data Comparison > Replication Data




                          Fig. B-210    Replication Data Dialog


                          By filling out this dialog, the clients to which articles shall be copied or trans-
                          ferred can be defined.
                          This menu can be accessed only by headquarters. The data can be trans-
                          ferred to the site in question. The advantage is that master data has to be en-
                          tered just once, at headquarters, to be distributed to individual or to all sites.
                          You can enter several lines here. Configuration of the Headquarters is done
                          with the system table xhaus.
                          In case of questions, please contact A+W.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Site Select the site (client) that is going to receive the data.
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artrepsteuer.hnr

                          Supply Type Enter the supply type for the selected site in this field.
                          Use <F9> to open the Supply types dialog. You can select a supply type there.
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artrepsteuer.beschaffnr

                          Deliv. Time If you have chosen Production in the Supply type field, you can
                          enter the production time in days for this client.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artrepsteuer.prodzeit

                          Supplier In this field you can select the supplier if the article is to be delivered.
                          One supply type must be Purchase.
                          Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artrepsteuer.stdlinr

                          Deliv. Time In this field, you can enter the delivery time in days if this article
                          is going to be delivered.

                          One supply type must be Purchase.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artrepsteuer.stdlz

                                       Product Identification
                                       Master Data > Article > <F4> > Product Identific. > Product Identific.




                                       Fig. B-211   Product Identification Dialog


                                       On this dialog, you can enter data for the legally required product code for this
                                       article. This will be printed on the product.
                                       These data can be analyzed in connection with the product code. The product
                                       code is a kind of text creation. Depending on the system configuration, these
                                       master data can be analyzed for text creation. The text normally appears on
                                       the spacer but can be printed on the paperwork as well on customer request.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       Article Shows the article number. The corresponding article name appears
                                       next to the field in plain text. You can select another article.

                                       selected country appears next to the field in plain text. The appropriate codes
                                       can be assigned via the Country (Codes > Market Partner) menu.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: artkenn.kfzcode

                                       Certification text You can enter the certification text in this field.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artkenn.ztext

                                       Rule w/o gas You can enter text for an IG unit without gas filling that should
                                       be included in the product code in this field.

                                       Rule with gas You can enter text for an IG unit with gas filling that should be
                                       included in the product code in this field.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artkenn.m_gas
