                          Technical details
                          Master Data > Article > Techn. Values tab > <Ctrl> + <F8>
                          Master Data > <F4> > Product name > Techn. Values




                          Fig. B-212   Techn. Values dialog - Header Data tab


                          There are various technical values that are not determined by the calculation
                          program based on the structure but have to be entered by hand for the prod-
                          uct. If the product is marked on the Techn. Values tab as relevant for the dec-
                          laration of performance, you can start this dialog directly from the Declaration
                          of Performance field with <Ctrl><F8>.
                          If no declaration of performance has been entered, the program will create a
                          new number. It consists of the contents of the ENV switch DOP_PRAEFIX + a
                          unique number that is determined in the :lenummer“ number range.

                             Field contents
                             All fields have to be filled in because this information will be printed on the
                             document.

                          Descriptions of fields

                          Declaration of Performance The stored declaration of performance is dis-
                          played in this field. If no declaration of performance has been entered, the pro-
                          gram will create a new number.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artikel.lenr

                          Description Description of the declaration of performance.
                          Technical info: alphanumeric fields, DB fields: arttechw.lebez

                Article                                                                Software Reference




                          Declared Services
                          Master Data > Article > Techn. Values tab > <Ctrl> + <F8> > <F2>
                          Master Data > Article > <F4> > Product name > Techn. Values > F2




                          Fig. B-213   Techn. Values dialog - Declared Services tab


                          The possible performances for printing the declaration of performance are list-
                          ed here. All fields that can be determined via the A+W SLT interface and the
                          external calculation program are marked with "*". All other fields can be main-
                          tained here manually. If the performance should be printed in the document, it
                          has to be checked in the checkbox as well.
                          The Load Resistance field is pre-populated with the glass thickness. For IG
                          units, the load resistance of up to three individual lites will be shown. The Load
                          Resistance field can be modified. The program will not check whether the new
                          entry matches the master data value.
                          All fields marked with (*) can be maintained by hand, of course. If the calcula-
                          tion through the calculation program is started later on however, manually
                          changed data will be changed.
                          Determination of the technical performances is started with the "Ext. Calcula-
                          tion" button or with <Start/F3>.
                          The dialog is described in detail in the Sales section.

                                       On this dialog, you maintain detailed information about the supply type of the

                          size is not met at document entry, A+W Enterprise will report this.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.pminb

                          this size is exceeded at document entry, A+W Enterprise will inform you ac-
                          cordingly.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.pmaxh

                          Minimum Height In this field, you can enter the minimum article height. If this
                          size is not met at document entry, A+W Enterprise will report this.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.pminh

                          Maximum Surface In this field, you can enter the maximum possible surface
                          of the article. If this size is exceeded at document entry, A+W Enterprise will
                          inform you accordingly.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.pmaxfl

                          Minimum Surface In this field, you can enter the minimum possible surface
                          of the article. If this size is not met at document entry, A+W Enterprise will re-
                          port this.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.pminfl

                          A+W Enterprise will inform you.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.pmaxsv

                          Minimum Aspect Ratio In this field, you can restrict the aspect ratio of an ar-
                          ticle to a minimum value. If this aspect ratio is not met at document entry, A+W
3.0 / 02-2023




                          Enterprise will issue a warning.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.pminsv



                B-384                                                        A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Article




                                       Rotatable Selection of this field depends on the configuration. Rotatable
                                       means that width and height of an article can be exchanged when checking
                                       the size restrictions.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.drehbar

                                       Description of the fields in the Prices section

                                       Cost calculation Entries in this field can be made only if the pricing module
                                       has been configured. This field defines whether the cost of the article to be
                                       produced should be calculated.
                                       It is analyzed only for BOM elements with Supply type Production. The head-
                                       er part in whose BOM the article is installed, must also have the Supply type
                                       Production. Please note that the supply type defined in the order will be ana-
                                       lyzed, not that defined in article master data.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • no:
                                            The BOM subpart is not evaluated in the cost calculation. The article BOM
                                            will be searched in descending order for other, cost-relevant articles.
                                       • yes:
                                            This BOM subpart is included in the cost calculation. Material costs will be
                                            calculated based on the production price list. The BOM of this article will
                                            not be searched for other, cost-relevant articles.
                                       • yes/next:
                                            The article costs are calculated based on the production price list. They are
                                            incorporated in the costs as an internal contribution margin. The article's
                                            BOM is searched in ascending order for additional cost-relevant articles.
                                       • Loss/next:
                                            The loss is analyzed for all BOM elements if the supply type is Production
                                            or Stock and if they are marked as Loss/next. Even the header part of the
                                            BOM will be analyzed if its Supply type is Production or Stock and is
                                            marked by Loss/next.
                                            For all articles that were marked with Loss/next, the individual losses are
                                            multiplied by each other. The losses for the individual articles are entered
                                            as percentages in the Material loss field.

                                             Articles with the supply type stock
                                             For a stock article, the BOM is never checked, regardless of which setting
                                             was selected here. Only the costs of the header article are used for cost
                                             calculation.

                                             Articles with the supply type purchase
                                             For purchased articles, the conditions of the allocated supplier are ana-
                                             lyzed. The calculated price contains all relevant sub-elements.

                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artmdzu.kostenkalk

                                       Loss (material) You can enter the loss of material for this article in percent
                                       here. The loss of material is meant as a general surcharge for quantity calcu-
3.0 / 02-2023




                                       lation. It can be applied at will, e.g. for waste.




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                       B-385
                Article                                                                Software Reference




                          The entry in this field is taken into account if material costs are calculated for
                          this article. A loss will be calculated when the article is produced or when stock
                          dimensions are withdrawn from stock.
                          The loss of material affects the quantity used to calculate the unit price based
                          on the quantity unit price.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.mverlust

                          Correct. factor The calculated loss for an article can be entered here. The
                          correction factor is meant as a general surcharge for pricing. It can be applied
                          at will, e.g. for waste.
                          When calculating prices at order entry, the calculated loss results in applica-
                          tion of the defined surcharge (in percent).
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.kverlust

                          Standard price The standard price for this article can be entered here. This
                          price can be used for individual transfer to financial accounting or for other, in-
                          dividual analyses.
                          Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: artmdzu.stdpreis

                          Type If you have entered a value in the Standard price field, enter the quantity
                          unit this price refers to.
                          The following options are available for selection:
                          • CU/piece:
                             Standard price per piece.
                          • CU/BQU:
                             The price is calculated per basic quantity unit (BQU), e.g. per square meter,
                             etc.
                          Technical info: toggle field, DB field: artmdzu.preistyp

                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                         B-391
                BOM                                                              Software Reference




                        BOM
                        Master Data > BOM
                        BOMs describe the individual elements of a product. These may be elements,
                        processing steps, or further BOMs.
                        A BOM is always based on an article, so that before entering a new BOM, the
                        article must be created. In the article master data, you can see from the BOM
                        field that a BOM is stored for the article in question.
                        This chapter provides information on the following subjects:
                        •   “BOM” on page B-393
                        •   “Formula editor” on page B-396
3.0 / 02-2023




                B-392                                                   A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                               BOM




                                       BOM
                                       Master Data > BOM or
                                       Master Data > Article > <F4> > BOM




                                       Fig. B-221   BOM


                                       On this dialog, you can enter the BOM elements for the selected article and
                                       change the first BOM level. Select yes in the BOM field for this purpose.
                                       These appear in the BOM editor at document entry.
                                       Use <F3> to load further resolution levels if the BOM articles include more
                                       BOM elements.
                                       To add more BOM elements to a BOM, use <F6> to add a new line.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       Article Shows the article number of the BOM element. You can choose an-
                                       other article number and thus change the BOM structure.
                                       This field appears in the BOM editor.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: strukt.sohn

                                       Description Shows the product name allocated to the article number.
                                       This field appears in the BOM editor.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: artikel.artbez1

                                       IP Shows the fitting position of the lites and foil layers (laminated glass).
                                       The assembly position is determined according to the following illustration.
3.0 / 02-2023




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                     B-393
                BOM                                                                  Software Reference




                        outside          inside


                              1 2 3 4




                        Fig. B-222   Examples of fitting positions


                        If there is no fitting position defined for LAMI foil layers, A+W Enterprise will
                        inform you accordingly; this will cause an error at document entry.
                        In system settings, you can define that the BOM must not be exited without
                        correction.
                        This field appears in the BOM editor.
                        Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: strukt.pos

                        Strct Defines the sense of pattern for patterned or ornamental glass.
                        The following options are available for selection:
                        • vert = vertical sense of pattern
                        • horiz = horizontal sense of pattern
                        • diag = diagonal sense of pattern
                        This field appears in the BOM editor.
                        Technical info: toggle field, DB field: strukt.strukthb

                        Qty1 Required quantity 1. For muntins, the number of vertical muntins is en-
                        tered here. For surface processings (e.g. edge grinding), the number of edges
                        is entered here; these are specified as width. For piece processings (e.g. drill-
                        ings), the number of processings is entered. Shapes require special attention
                        (edge allocation). This field appears in the BOM editor.
                        Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: strukt.anz1

                        Qty2 Required quantity 2. For muntins, the number of horizontal muntins is
                        entered here. For surface processings (e.g. edge grinding), the number of
                        edges is entered here; these are specified as height. For piece processings
                        (e.g. drillings), nothing is entered here. Shapes require special attention (edge
                        allocation). This field appears in the BOM editor.
                        Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: strukt.anz2

                        Styp Here you can enter the supply type for this article in the BOM.
                        This field appears in the BOM editor.
                        If you do not enter a supply type for this article in the BOM, the supply types
                        selected in the Supply type field will be applied.
                        Technical info: <F9>, DB field: strukt.bestellkz

                        FrNo Here you can enter the size inheritance formula for this article.
3.0 / 02-2023




                        Use <F9> to select a formula from the list.




                B-394                                                      A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                 BOM




                                       Use <F5> to open the Formula editor dialog where you can enter size inheri-
                                       tance formulas.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: strukt.erbkz

                                       Pr In this field, you select the documents on which the article shall be printed.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • Y:
                                          Print article on production and sales papers
                                       • N:
                                          Do not print article on production and sales papers
                                       • S:
                                          Print article only on sales documents.
                                       • P:
                                          Print article only on production papers.
                                       This field appears in the BOM editor.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: strukt.f_dru

                                       E/AP Exchange/additional part pricing. If an article is marked R or A, the arti-
                                       cle price will be considered for pricing, i.e. the article will be included.
                                       The following options are available for selection:
                                       • – (no selection):
                                          The price of this article will not be calculated separately but is included in
                                          the main article.
                                       • S:
                                          Article will be calculated according to the supplement price list
                                       • R:
                                          The price will be determined and calculated from the exchange price lists.
                                       This field appears in the BOM editor.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: strukt.azpreis
3.0 / 02-2023




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                       B-395
                BOM                                                                  Software Reference




                        Formula editor
                        Master Data > BOM > FrNo field > <F5>




                        Fig. B-223   Dimension Conversion


                        The Formula editor serves to enter formulas for calculating the article sizes.
                        These sizes will be inherited to all BOM elements.
                        If BOM elements should be calculated with a size calculation formula that dif-
                        fers from that of the main BOM element, you have to enter a new formula for
                        the element.

                           Exchange/additional articles
                           Size inheritance formulas will be kept for exchanged articles. If an article is
                           added, the system will use the formula defined in field Additional formula.

                        Descriptions of fields

                        Formla This field is pre-populated with entries from the field SiTr if a number
                        has been entered there.
                        You can choose another size formula for the article or enter a new number.
                        Technical info: <F9>, DB field: formel.ord

                        Name This field shows the name of the size formula. You can change it or en-
                        ter a new one.
                        Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: formel.bez

                        incl. Cutting Corr. In this field, you can select whether this article requires a
                        cutting correction. A cutting correction is an allowance per cut edge.
                        This may be useful for articles the edges of which shall be ground. The actual
                        article size is entered at document entry. A+W Enterprise will add the defined
                        cutting correction for production so that the finished article will have the or-
3.0 / 02-2023




                        dered size.
                        • Y:
                            Add cutting correction.


                B-396                                                      A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                  BOM




                                           Enter the sizes for the cutting correction in the Cutting correction field.
                                       •   N:
                                           The article will be cut with the defined size.
                                       If you are using a production management system, this entry is not necessary
                                       as this system will handle cutting correction anyway.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: formel.zkkz

                                       Offset red. Defines if an offset reduction can be applied to this article (e.g. in-
                                       side lite of an IG unit). The offset reduction formula has to be allocated to this
                                       article.
                                       • Y:
                                           Apply offset reduction.
                                       • N:
                                           Do not apply offset reduction.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: formel.stufkz

                                       $1 – $20 These fields show the formulas for calculating the variables. These
                                       variables are adopted from the Compulsory sizes dialog.
                                       New formulas have to be entered. You can leave this field only after entering
                                       a logical formula. Formulas will only be checked for obvious restrictions.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric fields, DB fields: formel.gv1 – formel.gv.20

                Product groups                                                               Software Reference




                                 Product groups
                                 Master Data > Product Groups
                                 The product group structure serves to organize products sensibly and clearly.
                                 For example, this helps you assign conditions and prices, with statistics and
                                 financial accounting, as well as in purchasing and discounting.
                                 This is why the assignment to a product group is mandatory for all products in
                                 the article master data. The product group is used for the assignment of con-
                                 ditions and in all sales statistics in which all sales are booked in product group
                                 oriented fashion.
                                 This chapter provides information on the following subjects:
                                 •   “Product groups” on page B-399
                                 •   “Individual product groups” on page B-401
                                 •   “Site-Specific Product Groups” on page B-402
3.0 / 02-2023




                B-398                                                               A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                       Product groups

                                       product groups.

                                       Short Name Short name of the product group.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: xxwargrp.kurzbez

                                       Details (Site) If you click this button, the site-specific details dialog opens.
                                        Software Reference, “Site-Specific Product Groups” on page B-402

                                    Finished Products
                                    Master Data > Finished Groups
                                    In this area, you can define customer-specific products.
                                    This chapter provides information on the following subjects:
                                    •   “Product Fixing” on page B-405
                                    •   “Product Set” on page B-406
3.0 / 02-2023




                B-404                                                               A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                       Finished Products




                                       Product Fixing
                                       Master Data > Finished Groups > Product Fixing




                                       Fig. B-227      Product Fixing


                                       If your customer regularly orders a product that deviates from the standard
                                       structure, this customer-specific special products can be stored here. The
                                       changed product structure can then be stored as a so-called fixed product in
                                       the article master data under its own number.
                                       This can reduce the effort required for entry during order creation since all
                                       changes to the standard product have already been made customer-specifi-
                                       cally.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       Cust Selection of the customer number. The name appears in the next field.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kauf.kunr

                                       (no heading) Selection of the order entry type.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kauf.eingang

                                       Project Selection of the project number. The name appears in the next field.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: kauf.objnr

                                             Lower dialog area
                                             The fields in the lower area of the dialog are identical to the fields for item

                                    Product Set
                                    Master Data > Finished Groups > Product Set




                                    Fig. B-228   Product Set


                                    On this dialog, you can enter one or several items with defined structure and/
                                    or size. In the document entry, this pre-defined product can be referenced. To
                                    do this, during item entry, enter the number of a set instead of an article num-
                                    ber. A+W Enterprise then enters the data from the pre-defined set into the doc-
                                    ument (order or quotation, for example) and queries the missing data. This is
                                    a special function that must be configured on request. For additional informa-
                                    tion, please contact a service employee of A+W Software GmbH.
                                    As creator of a product set, only customers can be selected who on the Market
                                    Partner Master Data > Private dialog have entered a value >0 in the first field

                                       Group Group number. Using this number, AWE functions such as calculation

                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                       B-413
                Field Configuration                                                                 Software Reference




                                      Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: kflddef.grpid

                                      SeqNo Sequence number. It has to be between 1 and 20, and must be
                                      unique. This sequence number defines the sequence of fields in transaction
                                      data. A gap in the sequence will cause a blank line between the fields in the
                                      transaction data menu later on.
                                      Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: kflddef.seqnr

                                      Label Label on the document dialog. It will be shownnext to the field in the
                                      transaction data.
                                      Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: kflddef.label

                                      you set the STYP to 2056, you can also define a header for a group of fields.
                                      Set the field in the sequence before the first field of the group and in Label, just
                                      store the desired group heading.
                                      Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: kflddef.styp

                                      mum length of the field.
                                      Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: kflddef.length

                                      Reference field In the reference field, a database field can be specified in
                                      the notation <tablename>.<columnname>. The configurable field will be pre-
                                      populated with the entry in this field. Please note that for kposprvfld you can
                                      only select database tables with field artnr as a key. For kaufprvfld you can use
                                      only tables with the keys mpnr and kuliflag. Sales fields are always pre-popu-
                                      lated from customer master data and purchasing fields, from supplier master
                                      data. Possibly existing projects will not be considered for pre-population. You
                                      can also enter a fixed default in this field. To make sure that the system real-
                                      izes that this is a default, the entry has to be preceded by a rhombus (e.g. #678
                                      for a long field or #ABC for a char field).
                                      Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: kflddef.reffield

                                      Priv. Field Here you can specify the number of a configurable field from the
                                      master data. For kposprvfld this is item master data and for kaufprvfld , market
                                      partner master data. This entry overrides the entry in the field Reference field.

                                       existing in the reference document will be adopted but data that makes refer-
                                       ence to the market partner in master data will be reloaded from the new part-
                                       ner's master data.
                                        For the reference entry MIT market partner change.
                                        For the reference entry without market partner change.

3.0 / 02-2023




                B-416                                                                 A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                       Commission




                                       Commission
                                       Master Data > Commissions
                                       Commission is considered even during order entry and calculated on the basis
                                       of product groups, customers, and time spans. For the invoicing or credit book-
                                       ing, the commission is booked order-related to a commission calculation table
                                       and logged (Sales > Sales > Comissions > Order Overview). A+W Enterprise
                                       enables commission calculations according to the following procedures:
                                       •     Standard procedure: a global commission key is stored in the system,
                                             which can be overwritten manually in the order.
                                       •     Representative/product group: Per representative and product group, it is
                                             possible to store a commission key in A+W Enterprise. The maintenance
                                             is done with the Commission Assignment menu item (Master Data > Com-
                                             missions > Commission Assignment).
                                       •     Customer: In the customer master data, a commission key can be stored
                                             for each customer.
                                       •     Time span: Depending on the contribution margin of the item, a commis-
                                             sion key is calculated. The maintenance is done with the Commission As-
                                             signment menu item (Master Data > Commissions > Commission
                                             Assignment).
                                       •     Time span/product group: Per product group, there can be a time span-ori-
                                             ented commission calculation.
                                       •     Customer/product group: Commission calculation is done customer-orient-
                                             ed per product group.
                                       •     Representative/customer: A product group-oriented commission calcula-
                                             tion can be set individually per representative (revenue representative).
                                       The setting of the appropriate commission calculation is permanently set in
                                       A+W Enterprise. If necessary, a change of the standard procedure can be
                                       made by A+W Enterprise Support.
                                       This chapter provides information on the following subjects:
                                       •     “Commission Code” on page B-418
                                       •     “Commission Assignment” on page B-419
3.0 / 02-2023




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                     B-417
                Commission                                                                Software Reference




                             Commission Code
                             Master Data > Commissions > Commission Code




                             Fig. B-233   Commissions Code

                             This way, it is possible that commission codes are used by the people entering

3.0 / 02-2023

                                  Text Management
                                  Master Data > Text Management
                                  In this area, basic data for the text generation within the document entry is de-
                                  fined. Variable and constant text passages and text formulas that are main-
                                  tained here appear later in the document entry, on production papers, and on
                                  customer-related documents. The texts thus have not just an informative, but
                                  also an advertising character and can influence business relationships.
                                  This chapter provides information on the following subjects:
                                  •   “Current Texts” on page B-421
                                  •   “Group Texts” on page B-422
                                  •   “Project Texts” on page B-423
                                  •   “Product Group Texts” on page B-424
                                  •   “Configurable Texts” on page B-425
                                  •   “Phrases” on page B-426
                                  •   “Variable Description” on page B-427
                                  •   “Text Formulas” on page B-428

                                       Current Texts
                                       Master Data > Text Management > Current Texts




                                       Fig. B-235   Current Texts


                                       On this dialog, texts can be stored that should be printed out on customer-
                                       bound paperwork. Use <F5> to determine on which forms the texts should be
                                       output. The selected forms are presented at the bottom edge of the window.

                                       Descriptions of fields

                                       File Name of the text file in which the texts are saved.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: akttxt.datei

                                       No For the case that several texts are provided within a single print item, this
                                       field can be used to specify the sequence.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: akttxt.lfdnr

                                       Printing pos. The printing position determines whether the specified text
                                       should be printed in the header, the footer or on the rump.
                                       Technical info: toggle field, DB field: akttxt.drupos

                                       Expiry date The texts stored are valid until the expiry date. Thus it is possi-
                                       ble, for example, to print Christmas greetings on correspondence until Decem-
                                       ber 14.
                                       Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: stammtxt.verfalldat

                B-428                                                             A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                 Costs




                                       Costs
                                       Master Data > Costs
                                       The organization of work can be done by cost units (e.g. manufacturing costs
                                       for product A, product B, etc.), by cost centers (e.g. costs of manufacturing,
                                       administration, sales) or by cost types (wages, salaries, write-offs, taxes, etc.).
                                       The system set up here to record work is not integrated into the commercial or
                                       production-technical areas. It serves only a manual entry of work, which is
                                       evaluated in the statistics area according to various points of view.
                                       This chapter provides information on the following subjects:
                                       •     “Cost Types” on page B-430
                                       •     “Cost Units” on page B-431
                                       •     “Cost Centers” on page B-432
3.0 / 02-2023




                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                        B-429
                Costs                                                             Software Reference




                        Cost Types
                        Master Data > Costs > Cost Types > Individual Descriptions
                        Master Data > Costs > Cost Types > All Descriptions




                        Fig. B-243   Cost Types


                        All cost types with their designation and details about the superior cost type
                        can be entered in a table here. A summary of particular cost types is possible
                        via the main cost type.

                           Multilingual names
                           Since QR2209, you can also store multilingual names in A+W Enterprise
                           for Cost Types.

                        Descriptions of fields

                        C type Display of the key number. To create a new cost type, enter the next
                        free number.
                        Technical info: numeric fields, DB fields: kart.kartnr

                        Lng Language ID.
                        Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xsprbez.sprkz

                B-430                                                    A+W Enterprise Master data
                Software Reference                                                                                Costs




                                       Cost Units
                                       Master Data > Costs > Cost Units > Individual Descriptions
                                       Master Data > Costs > Cost Units > All Descriptions




                                       Fig. B-244     Cost Units


                                       Products cause costs, which are booked via cost units.
                                       All cost units with their designation and details about the superior cost carrier
                                       can be entered in a table here. A summary of particular cost types is possible
                                       via the main cost type.

                                             Multilingual names
                                             Since QR2209, you can also store multilingual names in A+W Enterprise
                                             for Cost Units.

                                       Description of the fields

                                       C Unit Display of the key number. To create a new cost unit, select the next
                                       free entry.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: ktr.ktrnr

                                       Lng Language ID.
                                       Technical info: <F9>, DB field: xsprbez.sprkz

                                       Name Description of the cost unit.
                                       Technical info: alphanumeric field, DB field: ktr.bez

                A+W Enterprise Master data                                                                       B-431
                Costs                                                              Software Reference




                        Cost Centers
                        Master Data > Costs > Cost Centers > Cost Centers
                        Master Data > Costs > Cost Units > Individual Descriptions
                        Master Data > Costs > Cost Units > All Descriptions




                        Fig. B-245   Cost Centers


                        All offices at the company that cause costs due to service provision and use
                        are called cost centers. With the cost centers, an assignment of the costs as
                        they are incurred to the cost centers and thus cost-appropriate pricing is guar-
                        anteed.
                        The cost center and the name and details about the superior cost center are
                        listed in a table here. Via the main cost center field, an organization of cost
                        centers is possible.
3.0 / 02-2023

                                       is done here.
